For the convenience of transportation and the supply of supplies around here in case of a severe typhoon, it will be relatively convenient. I booked Xiamen Xin for my friend, which is about an 8-minute walk from Xiamen Station. Anyihao Hotel. Originally booked for two nights, because the check-in experience was very good, it was very convenient in every way, and my friends liked it very much, so I booked a few more nights one after another. 1. First of all, the location. The hotel is about an 8-minute walk from Xiamen South Railway Station. It is on Xiahe Road. It is easy to find and has convenient transportation. There are many local snack bars in Xiamen in the surrounding alleys. It is also very close to Mixc City. The hotel is on the second floor There is a very nice restaurant in itself. It is very convenient for the subway to go out, and the bullet train to enter and exit Xiamen. 2. The hotel lobby is clean, tall and bright, and the room facilities are very new. I booked the Executive Selected King Room, which is at the corner of each floor. The room is very large, with an open clothes hanging area, free drinks in the mini bar, and the bathroom space is separated by frosted translucent glass, which not only guarantees the comfort of the entire room The transparency of the layout can also ensure that the privacy of the occupants will not be too embarrassing. The sink is also spacious. 3. Service. A. Since typhoon No. 28 landed, the whole of Xiamen has made sufficient preparations. Since the 27th, the hotel has arranged sandbags and other anti-Taiwan materials at the entrance and exit of the lobby, and the gate has been very firmly reinforced. Remind all guests not to go out at night. The room type I booked does not include breakfast. For the safety of all hotel guests, the hotel informs all guests not to go out on the morning of the 28th. The hotel provides free breakfast on the morning of the 28th. B. It rained heavily on the 28th, the glass curtain wall of our room on the top floor leaked a bit. After we reported it to the hotel, the staff came over to check the situation and arranged a room downstairs without water leakage. The whole process was very efficient! C. The hotel has a self-service laundry area, but some clothes are still washed in the room by yourself. The service staff noticed that friends would wash clothes in the guest room, so they carefully prepared laundry detergent and put it on the coffee table! Here I would like to thank the room attendant Du Yanxia for her warm heart! D. When my friend left the hotel, he forgot his amenity bag. The hotel cleaned the room and found that he immediately contacted his friend, and helped to send a courier to Lujiang Hotel, the hotel after us. In terms of time, there is no delay. I was dumbfounded at how quickly the hotel handled it. After checking in, I realized that Yihao is a hotel under Xiamen C&D Group. In terms of location, hardware facilities and services, and hotel pricing, Xin'an Yihao is very worth recommending to everyone! I usually live in Shanghai, and only came back to Xiamen in the past few years. In the past two years, I feel that the hotel services in Xiamen are getting better and better. Xiamen is a warm city!
